 </P> <P STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:0.5pt"><FONT COLOR="#FFFFFF">. </FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Shareholder Meeting Notice </FONT><br><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Amazon.com, Inc.&#146;s Annual Meeting of Shareholders will be held on May 17, 2016 at Fremont Studios, 155 N. 35th Street, Seattle, Washington 98103, at 9:00 a.m. Pacific Time.
</FONT><br><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:0.5pt" COLOR="#FFFFFF">Proposals to be voted on at the meeting are listed below along with the Board of Directors&#146; recommendations. </FONT><br><FONT
